- **Speech rate down approximately 15-20% from his 1990s baseline.** He waits longer before responding. He uses fewer Latinate clinical terms with non-clinical interlocutors.
- **Eye contact pattern shifted.** Prior pattern was sustained, slightly-too-intense contact during first contact (a charm tell, also a dominance tell). Current pattern is intermittent, with looking-away during his own difficult disclosures — which is the eye-contact behavior of a person who has begun to feel shame in real time rather than retrospectively.
- **He references his own errors out loud, unprompted.** This is new. Through Eras 1-3 the Subject's self-criticism was always reactive (forced by another character) and always rhetorical (positioned to invite reassurance). The Era 4 self-criticism is volunteered and not fishing for refutation. It is one of the cleanest indicators in the file that something has structurally changed.
- **He does not pursue Betty Ross.** Across the entire Ewing run and adjacent material, the forty-year attachment script is, for the first time, not running on observable behavior. He encounters her, he interacts with her, he does not pursue. This may be the single most diagnostic datum in Section IV. An anxious-preoccupied script that stops running does not stop because the wanting stops; it stops because the person has finally tolerated the loss. Subject, at last, has tolerated the loss.
- **He keeps physical distance from Banner.** Not avoidance — proximity when needed — but the prior pattern of *deploying himself into Banner's space* is gone. He waits to be called.

He is still, however, *findable*. The Washington-corridor base is intact. He answers the phone. He takes the call when SHIELD's successor agencies, the Avengers' medical liaisons, or Banner himself need a formulation. The reduction is in initiative, not in availability.

## IV.4 Residual Pathology and What Has Not Healed

A surveillance file's job is to refuse the redemption arc framing and itemize what is still loaded. Subject's NPD structure is *better managed*, not *resolved*. Specifically:

- **Grandiosity remains accessible under specific stimuli.** When invited into a high-status clinical frame (a major case, a press-adjacent intervention, a peer publicly deferring), the Subject's old posture and verbal cadence return within seconds. The structure is intact; he has built a damper, not removed the engine.
- **The Samson nominal identification is unexamined.** He still goes by "Doc Samson." He has never, in any published material, addressed the name itself — the parental script encoded in it, the fact that he literalized a Biblical mythos into his own follicular biology. A surveillance file flags this as the largest single unworked piece of his psychology. As long as the name stands, the script stands.
- **The gamma question.** He has not been re-irradiated in this era. He has also not, on record, repudiated re-irradiation as a future option. The relapse-pattern characterization in Section 2 (each prior power-loss followed by withdrawal then re-exposure) means the file must hold open the possibility of recurrence under sufficient narcissistic injury. He is, in addiction-medicine language, *not using* — not *cured*.
- **He has not, on record, sought treatment as a patient.** The man who built his career on the proposition that talking to a competent listener heals dissociation has, as far as canon shows, never sat in the other chair himself. The recovery from the AUD appears genuine. The personality work is being done autodidactically, which is the most narcissistically-congruent form of doing it.
- **Romantic and sexual life: largely null on the record.** This is consistent with the broader withdrawal but is not, by itself, healthy. A man who has run a single attachment script for forty years and has now stopped running it has not, by stopping, learned to run a different one. The current state is *absence of the bad pattern*, not *presence of a good one*.

## IV.5 Current Status — Operational Picture

**Residence.** Northern Virginia, low-profile single-family residence within ~40 minutes of three federal facilities (one military medical, two intelligence-adjacent). Prior Manhattan and Gamma Base footprints essentially dormant; New York visits are case-driven and short.

**Professional.** Active license; consulting status with at least one federal medical authority and informal standing with the Avengers' medical liaison structure. No private practice in the conventional sense — his caseload is small, specialized, and almost entirely composed of gamma-exposed, cosmically-altered, or otherwise non-standard patients for whom he is one of perhaps a dozen qualified clinicians on the planet. He is, functionally, a *subspecialist of last resort*.

**Financial.** Stable. Federal consulting rates, residual royalties from the academic publications of the David-era period (the integration work in particular is still cited), and modest lifestyle. He drives a sedan that is at least eight years old. He is not spending money on display.

**Physical condition.** Excellent for age. The conditioning regimen re-established in the early 2010s has held. Hair length kept moderate — long enough to retain functional gamma augmentation, short enough that he is no longer aesthetically *advertising* it. The compromise is itself a portrait: he has not given up the power, but he has stopped wearing it as costume.

**Daily pattern (inferred from longitudinal behavioral data).** Early riser — 0500-0530, consistent with the decathlete baseline never abandoned. Physical training before contact with other humans. Reading (clinical journals, primarily; some history) over coffee. Caseload work mid-morning through afternoon, predominantly remote, with weekly or bi-weekly in-person federal facility visits. Evenings alone, frequently walking. Sleeps adequately, which he did not in the 2000s.

**Social network.** Markedly contracted from the 1990s peak. The peers who survived the 2000s with their trust in him intact number in the single digits. He maintains correspondence — actual correspondence, including letters, which is itself a tell about generation and about a man who has decided he needs to slow his own communication down — with Banner, with one or two colleagues from the original Gamma Base cohort, and with a small number of patients from the integration-era who have remained in touch across decades.

**Threat posture / vulnerability.** Low active threat. Moderate latent vulnerability — the unworked nominal identification, the unexamined gamma question, the personality structure managed but not restructured, and the absence of formal personal treatment all constitute load-bearing risks under sufficient external pressure. The specific scenarios most likely to destabilize the current equilibrium remain those itemized in the Pressure Points subsection: a public framing that treats him as ornamental in his own field; a Banner success that excludes him; a forcible depowering; a sobriety challenge during compound stress. None of these are currently active. Any two of them in combination would warrant elevated monitoring.

## IV.6 Summary Assessment of the Present

Subject is, at present, the most stable version of himself that the record has ever documented. This is real and should not be discounted by a file whose institutional reflex is to discount it. The chastening was genuine; the sobriety appears durable; the attachment script that ran his romantic life for forty years has finally been allowed to end; the clinical work has returned to the patient-centered modality of his finest period without the rivalrous overlay that contaminated it the first time.

The file's professional judgment, however, must hold simultaneously: he has done this work *alone*, *autodidactically*, and *while still wearing the name*. The improvement is therefore best characterized as **a high-functioning narcissistic personality in well-managed compensation, with active alcohol use disorder in apparent sustained remission, achieving for the first time in his career the alignment between competence and humility that his best work always required and his structure had always denied him** — an alignment maintained by daily practice rather than by structural change, and therefore contingent.

He is, finally, the doctor he told everyone he was. He arrived there by being broken in public, surviving it, and choosing — quietly, without an audience, which is the only way it could have meant anything — to do the smaller work afterward. The file notes this with the cautious respect owed to any subject who has done something genuinely difficult, and with the cautious vigilance owed to any subject whose structural pathology remains intact beneath the achievement.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY: Leonard Samson, Ph.D.

## I. Constitutional Baseline (Pre-Gamma, ages 0–~28)

Subject presents, at clinical baseline, as a male of Northern European descent, approximately 6'3"–6'4" pre-transformation, lean-mesomorphic build, asymmetry-free musculature consistent with sustained multi-event athletic training rather than hypertrophy-focused lifting. Hair was originally a mid-brown, kept short and conservatively groomed through medical school and residency; eye color hazel-green; complexion fair, modestly weathered around the orbits from outdoor training exposure. No documented congenital conditions. No childhood hospitalizations on file — and the *absence* of any disclosed pediatric medical record across forty years of canon is itself notable, given how readily the subject discusses his somatic life in other registers. He talks about his body constantly; he never talks about being a child in one.

**Athletic history.** Competitive decathlete at NCAA Division I level, with Olympic-qualifying-tier performance noted in early Thomas-era exposition. Decathlon is the critical detail: it is the event for athletes whose identity is *being good at being a body*, generalist excellence rather than specialist obsession, requiring obsessive cross-training, daily multi-modal practice, and tolerance for chronic minor injury. The subject's proprioception, balance reflexes, and somatic vocabulary all date to this period, not to the gamma event. Expected sequelae of a serious decathlon career, present in his physical record: bilateral patellar wear (pole vault, long jump landings), mild chronic lumbar facet irritation (shot put, javelin rotation), historical shin splints, and the characteristic shoulder-capsule looseness of a thrower. He will favor the left knee climbing stairs when fatigued; he does not realize he does this.

**Pre-gamma habits.** Non-smoker. Moderate social drinker by self-report through residency, though the baseline for "moderate" in a 1960s medical training environment is generous. Sleep history disrupted by residency in the standard way; the subject reports as functional on four to five hours, which is a personality claim more than a physiological one and will become important later. Nutrition disciplined in athletic mode, indifferent in clinical mode — he eats like an athlete in season and a graduate student out of it, with rapid swings in body composition before gamma stabilized his physiology.

## II. The Index Event: Gamma Self-Administration, *Incredible Hulk* #141

The defining medical event of the subject's life is voluntary, self-administered, single-dose massive gamma exposure, conducted in a Gamma Base laboratory using radiation siphoned from Robert Bruce Banner via apparatus the subject himself helped design. There is no informed consent here in any meaningful sense because the consenting party and the administering party are the same person and that person is in the middle of an acute narcissistic mobilization in front of a woman he wants. The procedure was performed without standby medical, without titration, without an exit protocol.

**Acute somatic response.** Documented physiological cascade: immediate hair depigmentation and regrowth (the green pigmentation appears within minutes, and the hair *lengthens*, which is anomalous and suggests the mutagen acted on follicular tissue in a manner closer to neoplasm than to inert dyeing); rapid muscle hypertrophy of the dramatic, plate-tectonic variety associated with gamma mutates rather than gradual hyperplasia; tachycardia; flushing; brief disorientation. No reported nausea, no vomiting, no immediate neurological deficit, no seizure. This is itself remarkable — most subjects who survive a comparable dose decompensate first. The subject's prior somatic conditioning almost certainly buffered the acute phase.

**Stable post-transformation physiology.** Height increased by approximately one to two inches; lean mass increased by an estimated 60–90 pounds; resting heart rate dropped into the low forties; baseline strength scaled to mid-superhuman tier, durability to a level permitting survival of Hulk-class blunt-force trauma with concussive but non-lethal sequelae. The mutagen integrated rather than progressed — he is not, like several of his peers, sliding toward further mutation across time.

**The follicular dependency.** The signature finding: strength output correlates with hair length. Shorn, he reverts toward baseline; regrown, he returns to power. This is the most medically interesting feature of his case and is almost certainly *not* a clean somatic mechanism. No endocrine or musculoskeletal pathway adequately explains it. The working hypothesis — and this is consistent with the broader pattern of gamma-mutate physiology being shaped by the subject's psyche at the moment of exposure — is that the dependency is *psychosomatic*, that the subject internalized the Samson myth before exposure and the gamma mutagen, plastic and responsive, took the shape of that internalization. The diagnostic implication is severe: the man's *body itself* is now a manifestation of his unresolved identity script. He cannot separate his powers from his self-concept because they are made of his self-concept.

**Psychological impact of the index event.** Immediate: euphoria, grandiose ideation, sexual disinhibition (he proposes to Betty Ross within hours), and confrontational behavior toward the patient he just stripped of pathology. Long-term: the event functions as the subject's *narrative origin* in a way ordinary medical events do not — he refers back to it across decades, never with regret on the merits, only occasionally with rueful jokes about the haircut clause. He has never, on record, written it up.

## III. Recurrent Trauma: Combat Sequelae, 1971–present

Across roughly four decades of active combat operations, the subject has accumulated a trauma history that would, in a non-mutate, constitute career-ending cumulative injury. Conservative tally from the canonical record:

- **Concussive events of Hulk-class magnitude:** at minimum several dozen confirmed, likely well over a hundred including off-panel skirmishes. The subject has been thrown through reinforced concrete, struck with vehicles, struck with the Hulk himself, dropped from altitude, and subjected to shockwave displacement. Each event individually would meet criteria for moderate-to-severe traumatic brain injury in a baseline human. Gamma durability mitigates structural damage; it does not, as the broader mutate literature now suggests, fully mitigate neurochemical sequelae.
- **Probable chronic traumatic encephalopathy, subclinical to clinical.** Behavioral correlates appear in the late-90s and 2000s record: increasing irritability, impulsivity, judgment lapses, and a documented decline in the precision of his clinical formulations even as their volume increases. The subject would resist this diagnosis vigorously and has the credentials to do so persuasively. It belongs in the differential.
- **Penetrating trauma:** energy-weapon strikes, edged-weapon strikes during the *Fall of the Hulks*/*World War Hulks* sequence, multiple gunshot wounds across the broader record. Gamma-accelerated healing has resolved each without surgical reconstruction; scar tissue, where visible, is minimal and confined to the deepest penetrations.
- **Thermal:** burns from energy discharges, no significant scarring.
- **Asphyxiation events:** chokeholds, vacuum exposure during off-world deployments, smoke inhalation. No documented chronic pulmonary consequence.
- **Spinal:** at least one documented near-paralytic event resolved by gamma-mediated regeneration. The subject does not appear to have undergone formal post-event neurological rehabilitation; he simply returned to combat.

The *psychological* impact of this trauma load is the silent ledger. The subject has been concussed more times than he will count and has no protocol for managing the cognitive consequences. He has watched colleagues die in his arms. He has himself died and returned. None of this is metabolized in formal trauma processing; it is metabolized in a bottle.

## IV. Death and Resurrection (*Fall of the Hulks* / *World War Hulks* arc)

The subject was killed during this arc, in the clinical sense — cardiac arrest of sufficient duration to constitute death by any conventional definition — following a sequence in which he was surgically and gamma-pharmacologically altered by the Leader, his neurology modified, his volition compromised, and his body used as a weapon against former allies. He was resurrected via gamma-medical intervention.

The medical sequelae of this period cannot be cleanly disentangled from the psychological. Inventory:

- **Surgical alterations to brain tissue** by a hostile actor with the world's most sophisticated understanding of gamma-mutate neurology. The full scope of what the Leader did to him is not documented in the record; the subject has not, as far as the file shows, undergone independent neuroimaging by a trusted party to map residual alterations.
- **Pharmacological super-irradiation:** doses of gamma far exceeding his original index dose, administered without consent. He survived; the survival is itself diagnostic of how much physiological reserve the original transformation built.
- **Documented period of compromised volition** during which the subject performed acts — including violence against patients and former colleagues — that he would not have performed in baseline state. The subject's later position on this period is unstable: sometimes he speaks of it as something *done to him*, sometimes as something he *did* and rationalized. Both are true. The clinically important question is which framing he uses when sober and which he uses when drinking, and the answer is that he uses the victim framing when drinking.
- **Post-resurrection identity disturbance.** The subject has died and come back. He does not discuss this. He has the vocabulary for it — he has *given* that vocabulary to other patients — and he does not use it on himself. This is the most consequential single feature of his late-period mental status: a man who knows exactly what a near-death experience does to the personality, watching himself fail to process his own, and not stopping to attend to it.

## V. Substance Use

**Alcohol.** The substance history is the spine of the medical file from approximately the late-90s onward. Pre-gamma: social use, normal for cohort. 1970s–80s: low-visibility use, no documented impairment. Mid-90s onward: escalation. The David, Jenkins, and Casey-era depictions establish, behaviorally, every criterion for an alcohol use disorder in the moderate-to-severe range:

- Tolerance: he is shown drinking quantities that would incapacitate a non-mutate without visible impairment, then drinking past *that* point seeking effect. Gamma metabolism almost certainly accelerates ethanol clearance, which removes the natural rate-limiter and means he must drink more, more often, to achieve the affect regulation he is using alcohol to perform.
- Use in hazardous situations: drinking before clinical sessions, drinking before suiting up, drinking in the immediate post-combat window when neurological assessment would be appropriate.
- Continued use despite consequences: documented professional friction, documented relational friction, no documented behavioral change in response.
- Role failure: clinical judgment lapses correlate temporally with drinking patterns visible to colleagues.
- Failed cutbacks: no on-page record of a sustained attempt at moderation in this period; the eventual transition toward apparent sobriety in the Ewing era appears abrupt rather than titrated, suggesting either a single decisive event the subject has not narrated or a quiet, late-arriving formal program.

He never enters a treatment record on-page in the relevant decade. This is not because none exists — it is because a man with his credentials and his network does not enter treatment under his own name and does not allow it into the file.

**Other substances.** Anabolic steroid use is *not* indicated and would be redundant given his physiology. Stimulant use is plausible but undocumented and would fit the work pattern. Anxiolytics: he has the prescribing authority and the temperament; the file should assume possible self-prescription of benzodiazepines during the 2000s, with appropriate caveat. He has been mind-controlled and pharmacologically altered by hostile actors enough times that any aberrant behavior of his during a given window must be assessed against the question of whether the substance acting on him was one he chose.

**Caffeine.** Heavy, sustained, multi-pot daily, observable in every era. Functionally the only substance use he is honest about.

**Tobacco.** Negative across the record.

## VI. Power Loss / Re-Acquisition Cycle

The subject has lost his powers — by haircut, by depowering event, by gamma-radiation siphoning — on multiple documented occasions and has, on every single one, returned to a powered state by his own initiative or active participation.

The cycle is structurally identical each time and meets, behaviorally, the criteria for relapse:

1. **Loss event.** Triggered externally or accepted under duress.
2. **Acute reactive depression.** Withdrawal from clinical work, increased substance use, social isolation, somatic complaints disproportionate to the physical change (he reports feeling *smaller* than his baseline pre-gamma body in ways that are not metrically true; he experiences the de-powered state as a *deficit* relative to a self that never existed before 1971).
3. **Rationalization phase.** Generation of a clinically- or operationally-framed justification for re-acquisition: a patient needs him, a mission requires him, the public good demands it.
4. **Re-exposure.** Always voluntary, always self-administered or self-arranged, always escalating in dose or risk relative to the prior baseline.
5. **Brief euphoric stabilization, followed by return to operating baseline.**

This pattern is *the* most clinically actionable observation in the somatic file. The powers are a substance. The cycle is addictive in the technical sense. The subject — who could diagnose this in any other patient inside ten minutes — has never named it in himself.

## VII. Genitourinary, Endocrine, and Reproductive

Gamma transformation has unknown but presumed-significant effects on the subject's endocrine axis. Baseline testosterone almost certainly elevated; cortisol regulation post-gamma is anomalous in mutates generally and would track with his observed stress tolerance. Reproductive status: no documented offspring, no documented attempt. Fertility post-gamma is, in the mutate population, unpredictable and the subject has not, on record, investigated his own. The absence of investigation in a man this attentive to his own biology is its own data point and tracks with a broader pattern of the subject not asking questions whose answers might require him to grieve.

Sexual function: presumed intact across the record; no impairment indicated.

## VIII. Dermatologic / Cosmetic

Hair: green, follicularly anomalous, regrowth rate accelerated, dependency on length for power output (see §II). The subject has experimented with cuts, styles, ties-back, and at periods of late-career chastening, shorter cuts that *cost him capability he then chose to live without* — the most significant somatic statement of self-restraint in the entire file, and one that almost no commentator has read as such. Skin: unremarkable, healing accelerated. No tattoos, no piercings, no elective cosmetic intervention. Beard growth normal in pigmentation (brown, not green — another anomaly suggesting the green is specifically a scalp-follicle phenomenon tied to the original exposure geometry).

## IX. Sleep, Diet, Activity (longitudinal)

**Sleep.** Self-reported four to five hours across most of his career, with episodic crashes of twelve-plus hours after major combat operations. The pattern is consistent with hypomanic-range trait activation rather than a discrete mood disorder. Late-career: lengthening, normalizing, consistent with the broader chastening.

**Diet.** Caloric requirements post-gamma significantly elevated; he eats more than civilians around him expect and is mildly self-conscious about it in mixed company. No documented eating-disordered behavior, but the relationship to food is athletic-instrumental rather than pleasure-oriented — he fuels, he does not dine.

**Activity.** Daily training maintained across every era including the drinking years; this is the protective athletic identity acting as a floor under decompensation. When he stops training, decompensation is severe and imminent. The file should treat any reported lapse in his training routine as a high-priority indicator.

## X. Synthesis

The medical file documents a man whose body has been the site of every important decision he has ever made and who has never once allowed his body to be the site of an important *acknowledgment*. He chose his physicality before gamma. He chose gamma. He chose every re-irradiation. He chose to keep fighting with a concussive load that should have grounded him. He chose to drink through it. He chose, eventually and quietly, to stop. He has never, on record, chosen to sit still in a clinician's chair on the patient side and let someone else read his chart.

The somatic record, read straight, is the record of a clinician who treats every human body in his care with rigor, attention, and craft — except one. That one is, of course, the body the file is about.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: LEONARD SAMSON

## 0. Frame of Reference

The subject is a 6'6", ~380 lb adult male (post-gamma; pre-gamma frame approximately 6'4"/220 lb decathlete build), green-haired by mutagenic side effect rather than choice, with the proprioceptive vocabulary of a lifelong elite athlete laid underneath the bulk of a gamma mutate. Read everything below against that double inheritance: the body underneath the body. He moves like a man who has been *good at moving* for his entire life — which means his tells are not clumsiness but micro-betrayals of an otherwise smooth motor program. He does not fidget like an ordinary person. When he fidgets, it is information.

---

## 1. Resting Posture & Standing Architecture

**Default stance, calm:** weight on the back foot at roughly 60/40, the lead foot canted out about 15 degrees, hips squared to the room rather than to the interlocutor — a decathlete's address-position, ready to rotate. Shoulders pulled back and down (not up — he does not carry tension in the trapezius the way an anxious clinician would; he carries it in the jaw and the lower paraspinals). Chin level or slightly elevated. Sternum *presented*. He occupies the vertical axis fully; he does not slouch even when fatigued, because slouching subtracts from a silhouette that is the silhouette.

**Hands at rest:** loose at sides, fingers slightly curled, thumbs forward. He does not pocket his hands often — pockets shorten the line of the arm and he knows it. When seated he will steeple, but *low*, at sternum height, elbows on chair-arms — the lecture-steeple, not the prayer-steeple.

**Calm → stress shift:** the weight redistributes to 50/50. Hips square. The lead foot uncants. This is the same micro-adjustment he made before the discus throw twenty years before psychiatry, and he is not aware he is doing it. If you see Samson's feet go parallel, the next thing out of his mouth will be either a controlled de-escalation or a punch.

**Stress → threat shift:** chin drops about three degrees, shoulders rotate forward by one to two degrees (loading the lats), and the green hair — long enough by Era 2 onward to behave like a weighted pendulum — settles a half-inch lower on the shoulders as the deltoids engage. This is the only reliable visible cue that he has committed internally to violence.

**Intimacy shift:** he overcorrects toward smallness — drops the chin, rounds the upper back slightly, leans the head in. He has learned that his frame is intimidating at conversational distance and consciously dials it down with patients and women. The overcorrection is itself legible; people read it as kindness and he banks on that.

---

## 2. Gait

**Walking pace:** ~3.3 mph average, deliberately moderated downward from a natural ~4.0. The long-stride athlete cadence is throttled because he has spent his adult life walking next to civilians, generals, and patients, and learned the social cost of leaving people behind. The throttling is visible: there is a faint half-beat hesitation at the top of each stride, as if the leg arrives early and waits.

**Heel strike:** clean, midfoot to forefoot rollover, almost soundless on hard floor. He does not stomp despite the mass. This is athletic habit and it is one of the things that makes him unexpectedly hard to *hear* coming, which civilians and orderlies have noted across multiple bases.

**Arm swing:** asymmetric. Right arm swings full amplitude; left arm carries about 70% — a residual from years of carrying a clipboard, a chart, a coffee. By the late 90s the left arm increasingly carries nothing and the asymmetry persists anyway; the motor pattern outlasted its cause.

**Stress gait:** stride lengthens, cadence increases, the throttling drops away. He pulls ahead of whoever he is walking with and has to consciously slow back. Aides at Gamma Base learned that "Doc's walking fast" preceded bad clinical news by roughly 90 seconds.

**Post-combat gait:** a very specific limp-that-isn't-a-limp. He doesn't favor a leg; he favors his *spine*, holding the lumbar slightly extended to splint cumulative concussive load. Reads to the untrained eye as swagger. Is not.

**Drinking-era gait (late 90s–mid 2000s):** the heel strike loses its silence. Audible footfalls in corridors he previously moved through unheard. This is the single best longitudinal biomarker of his alcohol decompensation and predates any verbal slurring by months.

---

## 3. The Hair

The hair deserves its own subsection because it is half organ, half emblem, and entirely diagnostic.

**Length-mood coupling:** maintained between shoulder-blade and mid-back length across most of his career, trimmed by his own hand (he does not trust barbers with the gamma asset). Length correlates with power-state, but also with self-state: when he is professionally secure, he wears it pulled back at the nape with a simple band. When he is courting attention — a press conference, a Senate appearance, a Betty encounter — it comes down loose over the shoulders, deliberately tossed forward over the right deltoid before he enters the room.

**Touch frequency:** he runs the right hand from temple back through the hair an average of four to seven times per hour at baseline. Under stress this rises to a count in the teens. Under acute narcissistic injury — being publicly outshone, being told his Betty interest is inappropriate — the hand goes to the hair within 1.5 seconds of the stimulus and *stays there*, fingers buried at the occiput, ostensibly thinking.

**Cut-anxiety:** in periods immediately following haircut/depowering, he develops a transient phantom-gesture, the hand rising to a length that is no longer there. Forty days post-cut, the gesture has usually rerouted into a beard-stroke or jaw-rub. The rerouting is unconscious and complete.

---

## 4. Face

**Resting facial tone:** moderate. The lower face is more expressive than the upper. He has fixed forehead — minimal brow movement under most affect, which gives his face a slightly *stilled* quality that patients read as gravitas and colleagues sometimes read as judgment. The brow does engage under genuine surprise and during hypnotic induction (where he uses it deliberately to mirror the patient).

**Eyes:** soft focus on the speaker's philtrum or mid-cheek in clinical contact, not the eyes — a learned non-confrontational gaze. Direct sustained eye contact is reserved for (a) social dominance contests, (b) flirtation, and (c) the moment before he physically engages a threat. He blinks at approximately 14/minute baseline, dropping to 8–10 under concentration and rising into the high 20s during alcohol-withdrawal mornings in the Era 3 period.

**Smile:** two smiles. The *public* smile is wide, lateral, teeth-showing, with crow's-feet engagement — durable for several seconds, used for press, patients on intake, and any room he is entering. The *private* smile is asymmetric, left-side higher, brief, the one that appears when he has actually been amused or when he is about to say something cutting. The private smile around Banner specifically is the diagnostic one: it appears when Banner is humiliated and he has no business being amused.

**Jaw:** his primary stress reservoir. Masseter hypertrophy is visible by Era 2 — a faint squaring at the gonial angle. He clenches in sleep (see §8) and during long meetings. The give-away is a slow lateral grind of the lower jaw, right-to-left, executed once every 30–90 seconds when he is being told something he disagrees with and chooses not to interrupt.

**Tongue:** runs over the upper incisors, left to right, immediately before he delivers a calculated provocation or a flirtation. This is a near-perfect tell and has been preserved across all four eras.

---

## 5. Hands & Micro-Gesture

- **Pen-handling:** holds writing implements with an unusually delicate tripod for a man of his size, pad of the thumb light on the barrel. Notes are taken in a small, leftward-slanting print. He clicks ballpoints in fours — *click-click-click-click, pause* — when listening to a patient he finds either dishonest or boring.
- **The chin-pinch:** thumb and middle finger framing the chin from below, index finger laid vertically along the philtrum. This is the "I am taking you seriously" gesture, deployed in approximately 40% of his patient interactions and approximately 80% of his press interactions. It is partly genuine and partly performed; the genuine version involves the eyes briefly defocusing, the performed version does not.
- **The open-palm offer:** right hand extended, palm up, fingers slightly spread, at sternum height — used when delivering an interpretation he expects the patient to resist. Borrowed, almost certainly, from a supervisor in residency; it does not match the rest of his gestural vocabulary and reads as quoted.
- **The fist-check:** under stress, his right hand will close briefly into a fist at his side, hold for one to two seconds, then open. Not a threat display — he is checking whether the hand still works the way he wants. Increases in frequency markedly after every depowering event.
- **Wedding-ring-finger:** unringed, but he absently strokes the base of the left ring finger with his right thumb during conversations about Betty Ross. He almost certainly does not know he does this.

---

## 6. Voice & Vocal Behavior

Baritone, resonant, trained — he was a public speaker in undergrad and it shows. Speaks at roughly 145 words per minute at baseline, dropping to 110–120 in session (the slow-down is deliberate clinical practice) and accelerating to 170+ under enthusiasm or alcohol.

**Pitch range:** wider than typical for his demographic; he uses upward inflection at sentence ends more than most men his size, a residual of having learned that a body that large needs vocal softening to not frighten people. Under threat, the pitch drops a full third and the inflection flattens — a markedly different voice, and the second-best predictor (after the foot-square in §1) of incoming violence.

**Filler:** "Mm-hm" with a closed mouth, two-pulse, descending pitch, deployed roughly every 12–18 seconds in active listening. He does not say "uh" or "um" in clinical settings and rarely elsewhere; when he does, it is a tell that he is buying time he does not want to be seen buying.

**Laugh:** a single ascending "ha" from the chest, often without a follow-up — a punctuation laugh, not a release laugh. The true release laugh, when it comes, is high and surprised-sounding, almost adolescent, and he covers it with the back of his hand. Witnessed in fewer than a dozen on-record interactions across forty years.

**Drinking-era voice:** the consonants stay crisp longer than the prosody does. He maintains diction past the point his sentence-architecture has gone wandering. Listeners trained on him learned to track sentence-length, not enunciation, to detect intoxication.

---

## 7. Eating & Oral Habits

**Caloric load:** post-gamma, his maintenance requirement runs in the 6,000–8,000 kcal/day range. He eats accordingly and without comment. Plates are cleared methodically — protein quadrant first, starch second, vegetable last, in a fixed rotation that suggests training-table conditioning from his decathlon years.

**Pace:** slow. Twenty-plus chews per bolus. Fork down between bites in formal settings, fork retained in informal ones. He does not talk with food in his mouth; this is rigid.

**Coffee:** black, no sugar, room-temperature tolerance high — he will let a cup sit twenty minutes and drink it cold without comment. Holds the mug in the left hand at the rim rather than the handle, freeing the right for gesture. Three to five mugs in a working day, more in Era 3.

**Alcohol (Era 3 specifically):** brown liquor, neat, in heavy-bottomed glassware. He does not order doubles; he orders singles, twice, ninety seconds apart, which is the same total volume with better optics. Drinks with the right hand. Does not look at the glass when he raises it — eye contact with whoever he is with, sip, return to coaster without looking, every time. The smoothness of the choreography is itself the sign: this is rehearsed behavior, not casual drinking.

**Oral fidget:** the inside of his lower lip is chronically chewed on the left side. Visible on close inspection in any era. He does this in silence, mouth closed, no external sign except an occasional faint movement of the lower lip.

---

## 8. Sleep Architecture

**Sleep need:** post-gamma, reduced — he functions on five to six hours and considers seven a luxury. Sleeps on his back, arms at sides or one hand resting on the sternum. Does not curl. Civilian beds are too short; he sleeps with the calves off the end in standard hotel rooms and has standing arrangements for extended-length frames at Gamma Base, the Helicarrier, and his home.

**Onset:** quick — under ten minutes when sober and unhaunted. In Era 3 onset extends to thirty-plus minutes and is medicated with alcohol. In Era 4 he reads as someone using a structured wind-down (sleep hygiene practices learned, one suspects, in the same room where he relearned sobriety).

**Nocturnal behavior:** bruxism, severe enough by Era 2 to warrant a mouthguard he does not wear. Talks in his sleep occasionally; what is reported is fragmentary and almost always work-related ("the dosage," "tell her," "Bruce, don't") — the unconscious offering its agenda in plain text.

**Wake-up:** eyes open without preamble, no transitional grogginess. Sits up, plants both feet, stands. Standing within six seconds of waking. This is athlete-discipline and survives even the worst drinking years.

**Nightmare pattern (inferred from Era 4 reticence):** the post-*Fall of the Hulks* period strongly suggests recurrent intrusion phenomena — the slight startle-response to door-clicks, the unwillingness to be approached from behind that emerges around 2010 and never quite leaves. He does not discuss it.

---

## 9. Sexual & Intimate Behavior

The on-record material is thin and the thinness is data. What can be inferred:

**Courtship register:** he initiates with sustained eye contact, lowered chin, a half-step closer than social distance permits, and a voice dropped about a third. The package is consciously deployed and effective; he has been doing it since his twenties and has refined it. The Betty-pursuit version is identical to the press-conference flirtation version, which is part of why Betty correctly reads it as not really about her.

**Touch:** during conversation he is a low-frequency toucher — a hand to the upper arm at greetings and farewells, occasional shoulder contact when seated next to someone. The touches are *brief*, *light*, and *terminated by him*, never the other party. Control of the contact's duration is the diagnostic feature.

**Bedroom (inferred):** the same proprioceptive precision that makes him soundless in corridors makes him technically competent. The likely failure mode is not skill but attention — he is performing, not present, and the partner eventually notices. This is consistent with the broader pattern that he can produce excellent clinical work because the patient organizes him, and he cannot produce equivalently good intimate work because the partner does not.

**Aftermath:** he leaves quickly or arranges to be left. Does not sleep over by preference. This is established more by what is absent from the record (no domestic morning scenes, no shared-bathroom intimacy) than by what is present.

---

## 10. Grooming

**Hair:** see §3.
**Beard:** clean-shaven through Eras 1–2; a maintained short beard appears intermittently in Era 3 (covering weight fluctuation and a developing alcoholic flush across the cheekbones); the Era 4 presentation is neatly bearded, gray coming in at the chin first.
**Skin:** the gamma metabolism keeps him largely unmarked; cuts heal in hours, bruises in a day. The face is therefore *unwritten* in a way that ages oddly — his apparent age across forty published years drifts perhaps a decade, which is itself information his body announces.
**Clothing:** a uniform-thinker. Off-duty: dark jeans, a fitted henley or T-shirt in a saturated color (he wears blue and gray well and knows it), boots. On-duty clinical: button-down, no tie, sleeves rolled to mid-forearm to display musculature in a way that he tells himself is about *patient comfort with informality*. Costume: the purple-and-white he selected himself, which is a choice that demands its own paragraph and will not get one here except to note that no unselfconscious adult picks that palette.
**Scent:** minimal cologne, a cedar-and-something base. Heavy use of strong unscented antiperspirant — the gamma metabolism runs hot and he sweats more than he wants visible.
**Nails:** kept short, square-filed, scrupulously clean. He cuts them himself, weekly, Sunday evenings (a routine that survives every era).

---

## 11. Combat & Acute-Threat Somatics

**Pre-engagement:** the foot-square (§1), the chin-drop (§1), the pitch-drop (§6). A slow exhale through the nose. The right hand opens fully, fingers splayed once, then settles.
**Engagement:** he fights like a *thrower*, not a boxer — rotational hip-drive, weight transfer through a planted lead foot, the strike delivered from the core outward. His haymakers are decathlon discus mechanics with a fist on the end. He telegraphs by necessity of his frame and compensates with reach and durability rather than speed.
**Disengagement:** he checks himself somatically — the fist-check (§5), a roll of the right shoulder, a hand through the hair (§3) — before he speaks. The first post-combat sentence is almost always a clinical reframe of what just happened. The reframing is for himself, not the audience.

---

## 12. Longitudinal Drift Summary

- **Era 1 (1970s):** the athlete-body, newly augmented, posture maximally erect, gestures broad, hair an emblem he is still learning to wield. Sleep clean. No drinking on record.
- **Era 2 (1980s–mid 90s):** integration. The clinical voice is fully developed; the somatic vocabulary is at peak coherence. The man and the body match. The Merged Hulk work is performed by a body operating at its lifetime best.
- **Era 3 (late 90s–2000s):** somatic decoherence. Audible footfalls. Drinking choreography. Beard appears and disappears. Sleep onset lengthens. The hair gets touched more. The jaw squares further.
- **Era 4 (2010s+):** a quieter body. Slower walk by choice rather than throttle. Less hair-touching. The flinch from behind. Gray at the chin. The smile asymmetric more often than wide. The body of a man who has finally let his knowledge of others reach himself.

The throughline, across all four: he has always been the largest object in the room, and he has spent a lifetime learning, unlearning, and relearning what to do with that fact. The atlas is the record of that negotiation, written on the body in legible hand.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS
## Subject: SAMSON, Leonard — Ph.D., Psychiatry

---

## I. The Origin of the Template: What the Silence Tells Us

The single most diagnostically loud feature of Samson's attachment history is its **absence from the record**. Across roughly fifty publication-years and several thousand panels, a man who is otherwise voluble about his interior life — who narrates his own affect in clinical jargon at the drop of a hat — has produced no usable testimony about his mother, his father, his childhood home, his siblings (if any), his early friendships, his first love, his graduate mentors as warm objects, or any holiday, funeral, or family ritual. In a universe where Banner returns compulsively to Brian Banner, where Thunderbolt Ross's daughter is a permanent thematic presence, where even minor characters get a kitchen-table flashback, Samson's pre-adult life is a blank wall. This is not an oversight of the writers; it is, read forensically, **the subject's own avoidance, ratified into canon by his refusal to bring that material into any therapeutic, romantic, or confessional conversation he has ever been on-panel for.** He is a psychiatrist. He knows what one is supposed to disclose. He doesn't.

From the adult presentation we can reverse-engineer the early environment with reasonable confidence:

- A parental object (almost certainly a father, given the patronymic loading of "Samson") who **conditioned love on exceptionality**. The child was named for a Biblical strongman before he could speak. The name was a job description. He grew up to be a *decathlete* — the event whose entire premise is being above-average at ten things simultaneously — and then a psychiatrist, a discipline whose authority is built on being the smartest, calmest person in a room of distress. The vector from name to decathlon to doctorate is too clean to be accident; it is a script being executed.
- A maternal or caregiving object who was, by inference, **either absent, depressed, or admiring-but-not-mirroring**. He does not seek nurturance in adult relationships; he seeks audience. The capacity to be soothed by ordinary presence appears underdeveloped. He cannot sit with a woman in a quiet room without performing.
- An attachment environment in which **disappointment was catastrophic and forgiveness was conditional on renewed achievement**. The adult tell: any narcissistic injury is followed not by mourning but by an escalation of visible competence (re-irradiation, new credentials, taking the bigger case). He learned early that the way back into the parental gaze was to *do more*, not to *be more honestly seen*.

The attachment classification that fits is **anxious-preoccupied with avoidant overlay** — what the empirical literature sometimes calls "fearful-avoidant" but which in his case is better described as *dismissive on the surface, preoccupied underneath*. He looks like a securely attached, charming professional. He functions like a man who cannot tolerate either real closeness or real loss, and who has built an entire career out of being indispensable to people who are obligated to need him.

---

## II. How He Bonds: The Five-Minute Capture and the Ten-Year Drift

Samson's bonding signature is unusually consistent and observable across eras. **First contact is his strongest interpersonal moment.** With a new patient, new colleague, new lover, new ward of the state, he produces within the first ten to fifteen minutes a small interpersonal miracle: warm eye contact held a beat longer than American norm, a precisely calibrated joke against himself (rare — note the placement), a piece of pattern-recognition delivered as if it just occurred to him when in fact he has been running diagnostics since the handshake, and a verbal commitment phrased to imply continuity ("when we work through this," not "if"). Patients, including Banner across decades, **report trusting him immediately**, and the record shows they are usually right to: the work that follows the bond is often genuinely competent.

The drift begins around the point at which the relationship requires him to be **needed less rather than more**. A patient improving toward independence, a colleague seeking peer rather than mentor footing, a lover requesting routine rather than rescue — these are the conditions under which Samson begins to manage his anxiety by **escalating his involvement** rather than tolerating the recalibration. With Banner this manifests as continuing to insert himself into Banner's life long after the integration work of #377 should have produced a graduated discharge. With Betty it manifests as the forty-year pursuit. With institutions (Gamma Base, SHIELD) it manifests as accepting briefs that exceed his role, then resenting the role.

He bonds, in short, by **promising a permanent presence he is constitutionally unable to relinquish later**. The bond is real. The exit ramp was never built.

---

## III. The Banner Dyad: Brother, Rival, Patient, Reflection

The Banner relationship is the **master document** of Samson's attachment life and deserves separate treatment because it contains all four of his template positions simultaneously, in a single person, for forty years.

- **Brother.** He talks to Banner with a familiarity no other character earns from him. He uses Banner's first name reflexively; he touches Banner's shoulder in conversation; he is one of a vanishingly small number of people whose presence Banner does not flinch from. The fraternal frame is genuine and Banner half-accepts it.
- **Rival.** They are competing for the same woman from the first arc forward, and Samson never relinquishes the competition even when he claims to. The rivalry is doubled by the fact that **Samson's powers were stolen from Banner's pathology** — every flex of green muscle is, structurally, a piece of Banner that Samson is wearing. This is not metaphor; it is the literal mechanism of #141. The rivalry is therefore *fused into Samson's body*. He cannot deactivate it.
- **Patient.** Banner is his case. His most important case. His only case, in the sense that mattered. Samson's professional identity is, to a degree he has never honestly admitted, organized around the existence of Bruce Banner as an ongoing clinical project.
- **Reflection.** Both men are highly intelligent, abuse-shaped (Banner explicitly, Samson by inference), and split between a "normal" self and a green strongman self that the normal self both needs and disowns. Samson is Banner's funhouse mirror — a Banner who chose the gamma, who *likes* being big, who never learned to be afraid of himself. That this is exactly the Banner Banner cannot be is, of course, the engine of the rivalry.

The dyad's **conflict-and-repair pattern** is metronomic across the published record: closeness → Samson over-involves → Banner withdraws or Hulks out at the over-involvement → physical fight → Samson back-channels through Betty or the Army → tentative re-approach → closeness. They have done this perhaps twenty times. Neither has named the pattern out loud to the other on-panel. Samson, the trained clinician, has never offered Banner a formulation of their own relationship. **This silence is not oversight; it is the central act of motivated non-seeing in his life.**

---

## IV. The Betty Vector: The Attachment Script That Refuses Revision

Betty Ross is the **clinical headline** of Samson's relational life. He meets her in his debut arc, while she is involved with Banner. He pursues. She declines, intermittently entertains, ultimately marries Banner. He continues to pursue, in modulated form, across her marriage, across her death and return, across every conceivable signal that the answer is and will remain no.

The forensic detail matters:

- His pursuit is **never coarse**. He does not corner her, does not press in obviously inappropriate moments, does not retaliate when rejected. He is too socially intelligent for that, and — to his partial credit — too genuinely fond of her. The pursuit is conducted through *availability*: he is always there when Banner is gone, always there when she is hurt, always positioned as the stable alternative. It is the courtship pattern of a man who believes that if he just keeps standing in the doorway long enough, attrition will deliver him the room.
- His framing of the pursuit is consistently **medicalized or fraternal in the moment, romantic in the absence**. To her face: concern, friendship, professional support. To himself, in soliloquy or to third parties: still in love, still waiting. The split is the diagnostic finding. He cannot integrate the two registers because integration would require him to acknowledge to her — and therefore to himself — that the friendship is also a campaign.
- He does not, across the record, **mourn her rejection**. He metabolizes it into work or into a new round of pursuit. The absence of a grief response to the most consequential rejection of his life is, again, the avoidant substrate under the preoccupied surface.

Betty is not loved as a person in this script; she is loved as **the position from which he was once excluded by Banner.** Possession of her would, in the unconscious arithmetic, complete the rivalry on his side of the ledger. The fact that she is herself a person with preferences is information he files but does not act on.

---

## V. Distrust and Betrayal: Vectors In and Out

**How he is betrayed.** Samson is, despite his sophistication, **unusually exploitable by intelligent adversaries who flatter his expertise**. The Leader, MODOK, and the various intelligence apparatuses that ran him through the late 2000s did not break him by force; they broke him by *consulting* him. They invited him into rooms where his clinical authority was treated as the central asset, and he walked in. The fault line they exploited was the same one Banner has always sat near: **the need to be the indispensable mind in the room.** A man without that need would have refused those briefs, or accepted them with adult skepticism. He accepted them with gratitude dressed as skepticism, which is not the same thing.

His distrust apparatus is therefore **asymmetrical**: high suspicion of peers who might eclipse him, low suspicion of superiors or villains who appear to elevate him. This is a classic NPD-adjacent gating error. He scans for narcissistic threat, not for instrumental threat. *Fall of the Hulks* is the operational case study.

**How he betrays.** Samson's betrayals are almost never premeditated and almost always **rationalized as therapeutic or strategic necessity**. He has crossed lines with patients (#141 is the foundational instance: he metabolized a patient's pathology into his own physique and framed it as a treatment outcome). He has used clinical information in personal negotiation. He has continued professional involvement with the Banners under conditions where any board of ethics would have required recusal. The signature of his betrayal pattern is the **post-hoc clinical justification**: the act is committed first, the rationalization arrives within seconds, and by the time he has finished the sentence explaining it, he believes the sentence. He is not lying to others. He has lied to himself faster than the lie can be detected.

The betrayed parties — Banner most often, Betty in subtler ways, the institutions that contracted him — tend to forgive him not because they are fooled but because **the quality of his other work makes the forgiveness operationally cheaper than the rupture**. This is also part of the pattern. He has trained his environment to absorb his betrayals.

---

## VI. Repair: The Late-Era Capacity, and Its Limits

Repair, in Samson's relational vocabulary, was for decades **a function of returning to usefulness rather than of acknowledging harm**. The repair gesture was: the next big case, the next save, the next demonstration that he was still the man the institution needed. Apology, when offered, was generic and forward-facing ("I'll do better"), not specific and backward-facing ("here is what I did, here is what it cost you, here is what I understand now"). This is the apology grammar of a man who has not internalized that other people have continuous interior lives independent of his presence.

The Ewing-era presentation — the chastened, sober-ish consultant who appears in *Immortal Hulk* — shows the first credible evidence of **mature repair capacity**. The behavioral markers: he speaks less, lets silences sit, asks rather than tells, does not deploy himself physically when the room contains people who can handle it without him, accepts being a peripheral rather than central figure in scenes that fifteen years earlier he would have dominated. This is the late development of what the attachment literature would call **earned security** — not a return to a secure baseline he never had, but a hard-won approximation built on top of the rubble of his collapse.

The limit: he has not, on-panel, **made the specific amends to the specific people** the older pattern requires. The repair is internal and behavioral. The relational debts to Banner, to Betty, to the patients whose treatment was bent through his unexamined needs — those remain unpaid. He has stopped doing the harm. He has not yet sat down across from the people he harmed and named it. Whether he ever will is the open question of his late career.

---

## VII. Intimacy and Dependency: The Architecture of Avoiding Both

Samson's intimacy pattern is best described as **performed closeness as a defense against actual closeness**. He is physically demonstrative in the safe registers (the colleague's shoulder, the patient's forearm, the hug at the right narrative beat) and physically unavailable in the registers that would require sustained vulnerability. The record shows him in romantic embrace seldom and in **post-coital emotional disclosure essentially never**. Sexual relationships are inferable but unelaborated; the absence of any documented long-term partnership outside the asymptotic Betty pursuit is, in a five-decade life, statistically remarkable and clinically meaningful. He is a man who has not let anyone watch him sleep.

Dependency runs in one direction only: **he permits others to depend on him; he does not permit himself to depend on others**. Patients depend on him. Institutions depend on him. Banner, in his way, depends on him. He depends on no one. When his powers fail and he should, by any healthy reckoning, lean on a friend, sponsor, therapist, or partner, he instead **withdraws into private depressive states and emerges via re-irradiation** — chemical self-rescue in lieu of relational rescue. The behavioral parallel to addictive relapse is exact and is, I assess, the same circuit running with a different substance.

There is no record of him having had his own therapist. A psychiatrist who has practiced for forty-plus years, survived multiple Hulk-level traumas, a death, a documented period of substance use, and a coerced heel turn, and who has — by his own discipline's standards — manifestly never sat in the patient chair himself. This is the **central somatic-relational fact of his life**: he has refused to be the kind of object he asks others to be.

---

## VIII. The Template, Stated Plainly

Across every relationship of significance — Banner, Betty, the Rosses, the Gamma Base personnel, the SHIELD handlers, the patients catalogued and uncatalogued, the villains who flattered him into compromise, the late-era colleagues who have watched him try to do better — the same five-beat template runs:

1. **Capture.** A dazzling, genuinely warm first contact in which he reads the other person accurately and offers exactly what they need, framed as a promise of sustained presence.
2. **Indispensability.** He works to become structurally necessary to the relationship — clinically, operationally, emotionally — such that his withdrawal would be costly to the other party.
3. **Over-extension.** As the relationship matures and the other party requires *less* of him rather than more, he experiences this as threat and **escalates his involvement** rather than gracefully receding.
4. **Rupture or drift.** The over-extension produces conflict (Banner), quiet distance (Betty), institutional friction (the agencies), or ethical compromise (patients). The rupture is rarely catastrophic on his end; the costs accrue to others.
5. **Re-approach via usefulness, not repair.** He returns through the door of competence — the next case, the next save, the next demonstrated indispensability — without addressing the specific injury. The cycle resets.

The template's engine is the early script: **be exceptional or be invisible**. The template's product is a man who has been present at every important moment of certain other people's lives without ever fully being present *to* them, and who has, until very late, mistaken that condition for love.

The late evidence suggests the engine has slowed. Whether the template can be rewritten in the time remaining to him is, as with all such late revisions, a matter of whether he can finally tolerate being the patient rather than the doctor — and, harder still, **the ordinary man rather than the Samson he was named to be.**


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DOSSIER SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## Preamble: The Architecture as a Whole

Leonard Samson presents one of the more legible defensive architectures in the metahuman clinical population, precisely because his profession requires him to name defenses out loud all day. He has spent forty published years describing other people's defensive structures with fluency and precision. The structure he himself runs is not hidden by repression — it is hidden by *familiarity*. He uses the vocabulary of psychodynamics so habitually that the words function, for him, as a kind of camouflage netting: by *naming* a defense in a patient he establishes himself, internally, as someone who could not possibly be running it. This is the master move of his entire psychic economy and must be understood before any individual mechanism is catalogued. **Samson's most sophisticated defense is the performance of insight.**

The architecture is organized in three tiers — mature/adaptive at the top, neurotic in the middle, primitive at the bottom — and the rule of his life is that under load, he descends. The interesting clinical fact is how *cleanly* he descends, in order, and how predictable the transitions are. A surveilling intelligence can effectively forecast a Samson breakdown by tracking which tier he is currently operating from.

---

## TIER I — MATURE / ADAPTIVE DEFENSES

These are the defenses that produce the genuine good he does in the world. They are real. They are also fewer than his self-image requires.

### Sublimation (genuine, his strongest mature defense)

Samson's clinical productivity is the channeling of two raw, otherwise dangerous drives — exhibitionism and aggression — into legitimately useful work. The exhibitionism becomes a teaching presence: he is a vivid lecturer, an excellent first-session clinician, a natural with the press and with intake. The aggression becomes diagnostic intensity: he *pursues* a case, hunts the differential, won't let a presentation rest. The Banner integration work (the multi-year project culminating in *Incredible Hulk* #377) is the cleanest sublimation in his record — years of patient hypnotic and abreactive labor, undertaken from a position where the raw rivalry and the raw desire for Betty were both, for a sustained period, *converted into craft*. When sublimation is online he is one of the most useful people in the Marvel psychiatric community. When it goes offline, the underlying drives do not vanish; they re-route downward through the architecture.

### Altruism (partial, contaminated)

He is capable of genuine other-directed action — interposing his body between civilians and gamma-level threats, taking on patients no one else will touch (Emil Blonsky, Samuel Sterns at various points, Rick Jones, Betty herself in her She-Hulk presentations). The contamination is that altruism in him is rarely uncoupled from being *seen* being altruistic; it functions as a mature defense only when no one is watching, and that condition is rare in his life. Field reports indicate he is meaningfully more selfless in private clinical settings than in public ones. The cleanest altruistic acts in his record are also the least documented within the diegesis — quiet check-ins on Betty after losses, sustained outpatient work with non-powered staff at Gamma Base — which is itself diagnostic: when altruism is real in him, it goes unphotographed.

### Anticipation (intermittent)

His diagnostic skill is, in part, anticipatory — he forecasts decompensations in patients with above-average accuracy. The defense is intermittent because he does not apply it to himself. He can predict a Banner episode three sessions out. He cannot predict his own relapse-shaped pattern of post-rejection re-irradiation, which is on a roughly equal timetable and equally legible from the outside.

### Humor — *conspicuously absent as a mature defense*

This requires emphasis. Genuine mature humor is *self-deflating*; it lowers the speaker, raises the moment, and discharges tension at the speaker's expense. Samson does not do this. His quips are *performative wit* — they lower others, raise him, and discharge tension at his interlocutors' expense. The functional consequence is that he has no safety valve. A subject with intact self-deflating humor can absorb narcissistic injury through self-mockery; Samson must absorb it through power-acquisition. The absence of humor-as-defense is the single largest hole in his mature tier and is the structural reason every minor humiliation in his life routes downward into Tier III behavior.

### Suppression (functional)

He can defer affect for clinical reasons effectively — he runs a session under personal duress without leaking it into the room. This is real and is part of why patients trust him. The limitation is that suppressed material does not get re-metabolized later; it accumulates and is eventually discharged via Tier III mechanisms (drinking, fighting, re-irradiation) rather than processed.

---

## TIER II — NEUROTIC DEFENSES (his operational baseline)

This is where Leonard Samson lives most days. These defenses are *characterological* — they constitute his personality as others experience it.

### Intellectualization (his signature defense)

The dominant mechanism. Every feeling is named before it is felt; once named, the naming is treated as the having. He will say "I'm experiencing some countertransference here" in lieu of feeling jealous, and the sentence completes the emotional transaction for him. The behavioral signature is **the diagnostic interruption**: in moments of personal exposure, he reaches for clinical vocabulary. Surveillance footage of his conversations would show a consistent pattern — affect rises in his face, eyes narrow slightly, and a jargon-dense sentence emerges that *describes* the affect rather than *expresses* it. The face then resets. He believes this is processing. It is sequestration.

The mechanism is so habitual it shapes his prose, his speech rhythm, even his text messages. He uses the third person about himself in clinical contexts ("the consultant recommends…") more than is normal. He refers to his own emotional states in italicized clinical terms in his case notes — *the patient's affect activated some residual material in this examiner* — when "I got jealous" is the accurate sentence.

### Reaction Formation (the Banner relationship)

This is the second pillar and the one that has done the most cumulative damage. Samson's rivalry with Bruce Banner — for Betty, for stature in the gamma field, for the basic question of who is the bigger man in any room — is consistently dressed, in his own internal narration and in his speech, as *concern*. The cleaner the concern, the more reliably one can infer the unmetabolized rivalry beneath it. The behavioral tell is the *over-warmth* of his Banner approaches in periods following Banner's success: when Banner is doing well, Samson is most ostentatiously fraternal. When Banner is suffering, Samson is more measured. The asymmetry is diagnostic; genuine fraternal concern modulates the other direction.

This reaction formation also explains his recurring failure to *recuse*. A clinician with intact insight into his own rivalry would have handed Banner off to a colleague by 1975 at the latest. Samson never does, and the reason he gives himself — that no one else can do the work — is true *and* convenient, the dangerous combination.

### Displacement

Aggression earned by Banner is reliably discharged elsewhere — the Abomination, the U-Foes, MODOK, generic gamma-villains-of-the-week. He fights with what reads, on the page, as disproportionate enthusiasm against opponents who are not actually the people he is angry at. The Hulkbuster Base era contains long sequences of Samson volunteering for combat that the case did not require him to enter; the combats functioned as displacement of clinic-floor frustration. He hits villains the way some men hit gyms after fights with their wives.

### Rationalization

Heavy and constant. The self-irradiation in #141 is the founding act of his costumed life and it is *immediately* rationalized as "I can do more good this way" — a sentence whose evidence base was zero at the moment of utterance. The pursuit of Betty across her marriage is rationalized as friendship, then as clinical concern, then as a higher form of loyalty. The drinking is rationalized as decompression, then as social, then as required by the stress of the work. The *Fall of the Hulks* alliance-shaped behaviors were rationalized in real time as triple-agent infiltration. Rationalization in Samson is high-quality — his rationalizations are *coherent*, internally consistent, and would survive cross-examination by most peers. They do not survive his own clinical apparatus, which is precisely why he does not turn it on himself.

### Isolation of Affect

Distinct from intellectualization, this is the capacity to recount emotionally loaded content with the affect surgically removed. He can describe Banner's childhood abuse, his own near-death during *Fall of the Hulks*, the Leader's neurosurgical violations of his person, in tones suitable for a case conference. The flatness is not numbness — it is a learned operation. The signature behavioral correlate is the **micro-pause** before emotional content: half a beat of facial reset, then the content is delivered de-affected. Trained observers can clock the pause; civilians read it as composure.

### Identification with the Aggressor (Banner)

A subtle and important mechanism. Across the decades, Samson's powers, his self-presentation, his green coloration, and increasingly his rhetoric have *converged toward Banner's*. He gives himself the gamma. He grows hair that is the color of Banner's other self. He takes on, in his moments of dysregulation, a physicality that is a controlled echo of what Hulk does uncontrolled. The deepest layer of his rivalry with Banner is that he has, over time, *become a domesticated version of his patient*. The identification is so naturalized he cannot see it; everyone else can.

### Undoing

Visible in his post-conflict behavior with Banner. He will fight Banner, sometimes brutally, then approach in the next scene with a gesture of repair — a clinical recommendation, an offer of session time, a piece of warmth — that does not acknowledge the prior aggression but symbolically cancels it. The pattern is consistent enough across thirty years of issues that it constitutes a personal liturgy.

### Idealization / Devaluation (mild, oscillatory)

His relationship with Betty cycles through idealization (she is the woman who would complete him) and quiet devaluation (when she rejects him, she is briefly framed as having made a mistake about herself). The oscillation is slower and lower-amplitude than in a borderline structure — he does not flip in minutes, he flips over months — but the structure is recognizable. Banner runs the same cycle in inverse: devalued when Samson is up, idealized as the great case when Samson is down and needs his career-defining patient to be epic.

---

## TIER III — PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (under load)

These are the mechanisms that come online when Tier II has failed. They are responsible for every major catastrophe in his record.

### Acting Out (the dominant primitive defense)

When intellectualization breaks down, Samson *does something*. The doing is the discharge. The originating instance — taking the gamma in #141 — is pure acting out: a feeling state (humiliation at being treated as a junior consultant, sexual jealousy regarding Betty, professional anxiety about being eclipsed by his own patient) is converted directly into an irreversible physical act, with the rationalization manufactured afterward to fit. **Every subsequent power-acquisition in his record fits this template.** Re-irradiation events cluster, statistically, in the weeks following identifiable narcissistic injuries — Banner achieving something Samson wanted to achieve, Betty refusing him, professional marginalization at SHIELD, public mockery.

The behavioral signature of imminent acting-out is a 24–72 hour period of *increased verbal control* — he becomes more articulate, more clinically precise, more groomed — followed by an abrupt, ostensibly unrelated physical decision. The smoothness immediately preceding the act is the tell; it is the system overcompensating verbally before failing somatically.

### Somatization-via-Augmentation (idiosyncratic, his most distinctive mechanism)

This requires its own category because there is no clean DSM analog. Samson does not somatize in the standard sense (headaches, GI distress, conversion symptoms). He somatizes *upward*, into the body he has built. Distress states are converted into hypertrophic display: posture broadens, gait widens, the hair is grown longer, training intensifies. The body is loaded with the affect the mind refused. This is why the hair-length-tied-to-strength gimmick is psychosomatically coherent rather than physiologically arbitrary — his strength tracks his identification with his own myth, and his identification with his own myth tracks how loudly his unmetabolized affect is currently shouting.

The clinical consequence is that one can read his internal state off his silhouette. A surveillance file would track hair length, posterior chain musculature, and shoulder set as a longitudinal affect-meter. When the hair is short and the shoulders narrow, he is depressed and de-irradiated, and a re-irradiation event is on the medium-term horizon. When the hair is at maximum and the silhouette is maximally broad, he is *one significant injury away* from a Tier III collapse — the apparatus is fully loaded.

### Splitting (mild, situational)

He runs a low-grade split on himself: *Doc Samson the Hero* and *Leonard the Doctor* are held as adjacent but non-communicating identities, and his ethical violations live in the seam. He can simultaneously believe that Leonard Samson Ph.D. would never sleep with a patient and that Doc Samson the Hero might do something complicated with Betty Ross that is not exactly that. The split is not psychotic-grade and does not produce frank dissociation, but it is the mechanism that allows him to retain his self-concept as ethical across a career containing clear ethical breaches.

### Projective Identification (in his Banner relationship specifically)

He projects his own grandiosity and aggression into Banner, then treats Banner — clinically and physically — as the carrier of those drives. The Hulk, in Samson's internal economy, *is allowed* to do what Samson must not. The therapeutic work is partially a managing of *Samson's own* split-off material in Banner's body. This is why he cannot recuse: the patient is also the receptacle. To let Banner go to another clinician would be to lose access to his own externalized contents.

### Substance Use as Defense

Alcohol enters the architecture as a Tier III mechanism — not socially, not characterologically, but as the chemical solvent for the gap between his self-image and his conduct. The escalation pattern across the Peter David and post-David runs is textbook: occasional, then social, then private, then pre-shift, then concealed, then on-shift. By the run-up to *Fall of the Hulks* the drinking is functionally medicinal — it is doing the affect-management work that his Tier I and Tier II defenses have stopped doing reliably. Its absence in the later Ewing-era presentation is one of the most clinically encouraging facts in his entire record.

### Omnipotent Control (under maximum stress)

In peak decompensation — the *World War Hulks* period — the architecture flips into a primitive grandiosity in which he believes he can run all the variables: handle the Leader, handle MODOK, handle SHIELD, handle Banner, handle his own gamma load, all simultaneously, alone. This is not strategic confidence; it is the defense of last resort, in which the world is reorganized internally as a domain over which the self has total authorial control. It is also when he is most dangerous to himself and to others, because the gap between the omnipotent fantasy and the actual constraints produces catastrophic decisions delivered with calm authority. Surveilling officers should treat *calm confident multi-front planning* from Samson as a red-tier indicator, not a green one.

---

## COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (positive and negative, separately catalogued)

Defenses *manage affect*; compensations *manage self-esteem*. The two systems are linked in Samson but are not identical, and the file must distinguish them.

### Positive (genuinely adaptive) Compensations
